<time>1559239322979< /time><rating>5</rating>< review>
This is my favorite local yoga studio. The environment is very chill, grounded and the instructors are supportive. There are other yoga studios in Midtown that feel pretentious, cult-y...this is not one of those studios. I love this place.

For more rigorous classes, choose these instructors: Blake, Jany, Rachel, Janna, Evey and Stephanie.
For more strength building, choose these instructors: Jamie, Taylor, Ellen and Amanda.

Every instructor is unique...some classes I will burn 300 calories, others I only burn 150. Keep that in mind...every class is different, week to week!

I love this place so much.< /review>

< Text>
It‚Äôs wonderful. The staff, teachers, and classes are awesome. I had never done yoga in a guided class before. So, naturally, I was nervous. I didn‚Äôt think I‚Äôd literally be able to handle the heat (of their Vinyasa classes) or keep up with the double zeros. They make you feel comfortable. They also challenge you but reiterate that it‚Äôs about going at your own pace. I was initially wary too since I have a permanent hip injury. The teachers are more than happy to provide modifications if need be. I like that they practice what they preach. If you‚Äôre wary, like I was, start with their $30 for 30 days (keep in mind it‚Äôs consecutive). They have lots of classes to choose from, hot and regular. I am no longer wary and now an unlimited monthly member! Not only will you make Yoga practice a part of your daily routine but also your lifestyle. Granted, it‚Äôs an expensive hobby but it‚Äôs definitely worth it for your mental and physical health. There are few things in life that give you what you truly need; a healthy body (and heart) and happy mind. And I‚Äôd recommend Solfire yoga as one of the few.</Text>

<gmapID>0x809ad0c053012119:0x4b8a14f3c57bd81e<//gmapID>< review>
I like the fact your community offers classes like Kundalini Yoga, Yin, and Nidra. I find those classes more difficult to access in other studios in Sacramento.  These classes offer great variety for people who get stuck in energy patterns and who are overly structured. I also like that your studio has a private meditation room with bowls and oracle cards. I do not know of any other studio that has that. The quotes that you leave on our shoes are also a great idea because it is an opportunity for people to leave the class with the sense of accomplishment and good luck. The Karma yoga (selfless service volunteering) is also a great system for people who are willing and capable to contribute to the community with the best of their abilities.All in all, solfire yoga is a great place to practice yogic techniques and are open to people who face difficulties with life.< /review>

Amanda S< /name>

1481561842792</Time>
<Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
Visited some wineries this weekend while on vacation and Starmont was hands down the best winery I went to all weekend. The staff were very knowledgeable and friendly, the location was convenient, the tasting room and seating area was beautiful, and the wines were fantastic. They have a really lovely fire pit area with comfortable couches and chairs and even blankets you can use if you get a bit chilly. What really made the difference in my mind was the staff. They were really accommodating and just good people all around. Some of the other places we went to, people were a bit snobbish and it felt like they could care less whether you were there or not. I highly recommend the GSM blend and their Chardonnay. Both were pretty fantastic in my opinion.</Review>

< name>
Matthew Frith<//name>
<Date>1487492541210< /Date><Rating>2< /Rating>< text>
Perhaps I went on a bad day... we arrived around 2pm on a Saturday. We often frequent Napa and Sonoma to pick up our wine club selections and have always noticed starmont when coming in and figured we would try it this time around.We walked in and noticed it was fairly crowded. There is a lot of seating inside of the tasting room and every seat was taken, there was plenty of room at the wine bar though. We walked up and waited patiently. There were 3 workers behind the counter and we waited around 10 minutes and was not acknowledged once. There were 2 other couples there, so I feel that there was at least some time to say we will be with you in a bit or at least a hello... but we sat there and waited. This gave us the opportunity to look around at the crowd. It was a pretty young crowd. Everyone seemed to be 21, which is fine, but it was rather loud and you could hear the random "OMG" once in awhile, similar to a bar. This environment reminded me of my college days and although it was only 6 years ago, it is something that I want nothing to do with. There was even a girl taking multiple selfies, sipping wine and posting it on snapchat. I am a former wine buyer and was disappointed that I was not able to try their wines, but the environment was very off setting. If this place wants to cater to this crowd, that is fine. This review is more aimed at those who want a relaxing environment and, frankly, want semi-decent customer service. If you just turned 21 or are new to wine, then this is the place for you.</text>

<date>1600637236367< /date><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Great tasting, freshly grilled Mediterranean food, at a reasonable price point, in Vernon? Yep!

This is a franchise and you'd be skeptical that all are the same, but so far the Commerce, Vernon and Long Beach locations have not disappointed. The recipes are seemingly the same across the board, and service had been courteous and fast at all.

I personally recommend the chicken kebabs (and I'm typically beef all the way in any setting but the chicken kebab is exceptionally well seasoned).

Don't overlook the family deals as well, great value.</Review>

<name>Matt Arrington</name><review>I don't usually leave reviews online, but my experience here was so poor I felt obliged to warn others. I booked a room here for a weekend getaway with my girl friend, for Friday and Saturday night last February, 2021. With tax the room came out to $400.00 a night. Pricey, but it is close to the water, and the pictured rooms looked decent.

The room we stayed in was dark, poorly lit, and didn't have enough windows. Right off when we got in to the room we noticed a loud squeal coming from the walls, and this was 9:30 at night. It sounded like it was coming from laundry equipment that ran constantly throughout our stay. There was also an ice machine outside that had a loud fan that kept turning on and off all night. I never thought of ice machines being loud before this, but this one was. The walls seemed to be paper thin, and we could clearly hear conversations going on in the office next door. It was early in the morning, when I asked them if they could keep it down, and they just kept chatting it up, as if we never even asked. There was a ton of foot traffic in front of the room as people were checking in / out. The bathroom sink was outside the bathroom, and shoved in to a corner in the main bedroom, which was just plain weird. The last straw for me was when we ran out of toilet paper.

We asked for a different room, and they refused to move us. They refused to give any discount or refund. His argument for not giving money back was that room quality was "subjective" which I just found insulting given how bad the room was. He was willing to give us a discount on a future stay, and he admitted to having better rooms, but after such a bad experience no way I am going back there and giving them any more of my money.

< review>
I am beyond words for how we have been treated and taken care of during our unexpected stay at Casablanca Inn. We were evacuated from our home in Felton due to the fires, and all the hotels we found were booked and unwilling to help. We are locals here and have never stayed near the wharf. After a lot of searching, we finally came across Casablanca Inn and gave them a call. They were sympathetic, made a room available, let us pay night by night, extended our parking passes, and so much more to help in this unsure time. The staff was friendly, the room was clean and the beds were super comfy. We had our own patio with an ocean view. They are not only pet friendly, but they are pet forward :) They never asked me what kind of dog I had or what his temperament was (I have a 70lb pitbull btw) they greeted my dog as well and they have an outdoor enclosed potty area for them with poop bags and a garbage can. Lastly, they gave us a huge local evacuee discount was made things a little easier to deal with. Thank you Casablanca Inn and staff for all you did for us the past few days. This will now be an annual stay for us going forward!< /review>

We were just here one night, but our stay was nice. I saw a number of reviews that complained about this property, but we like it. It is a historic property, but everything I saw was nicely updated and maintained. I had two small complaints. We were in one of the rooms near beach drive. The noise was not an issue, but the distance to the parking lot is crazy. I had to carry everything up four flights of stairs and walk a good distance to the lot. The smaller window only has blinds,and very bright lights outside. My room was as bright as midday all night. It would be nice to have curtains on that window.</Review>

< text>
We booked this hotel a month and a half before our arrival because it was across the street from the beach and the room we reserved could accommodate our adult family of four with the room description of:  "Family Suite
Description: Sleeps six comfortably - Private King Bed and Queen bedrooms, a Queen Sofa Bed, a full kitchen along with a dining area. Guests have access to two bathrooms including one tub."  We got there and our room was not ready.  They took our number and told us they'd call us when the room was ready.  They did not call us on the phone number they asked us for.  We checked in and went to our room to find an open room with 2 queen beds and two camper like seats that "could be" used as beds, I guess and only one bathroom.  When we went to tell the desk clerk that we received the wrong room, he stated that this has happened before and he would refund our money.  What?  We just want the room we paid for.  We were told that is not an option as they had given "that" room to someone else and the owner/management have now categorized this new open room as a family suite even though the description does not come close to what we booked.  They had another room available (a king bed with a pull out couch) but instead of offering that to us in addition to what we had they told us that we could switch to that room but could not have it in addition to the room they were trying to give us. I pointed out that if they gave us that additional room, we would then have the 2 queen beds, king bed and 2 baths we had paid for but we were told that they would not do that for us.  They did nothing to try to accommodate us.  I will never go to this hotel again and I urge everyone reading reviews to reconsider this hotel.  We ended up going to the Paradox Autograph Collection Hotel and really enjoyed it!  Not on the beach but the accommodations made up for that.<//text>

< review>
We had nothing but positive experiences when staying with Casablanca Inn. We booked a family room (One king bed & a pull out) for myself, my boyfriend and best friend. When we arrived at 9pm, exhausted from a huge drive, they upgraded us at no extra cost to an ocean view room with two queen beds. The rooms were clean, well presented and had a beautiful view of the beach. The front desk staff were extremely helpful, knowledgeable and lovely to speak with. The following day they offered us a late check out which was really convenient for us. After our departure, we realized we had left some medication in the room, after I called up and spoke with Will at the front desk, they agreed to mail it out to us as we were already 3.5 hours away. I received a phone call from Brian the day after confirming that he had express posted it out to us to make sure it arrived in time before we flew back home to Australia. I have never received such positive service from a hotel before. They truly went above & beyond to make sure I was happy and I am so appreciative. I highly recommend their services for anyone staying in Santa Cruz as it is a short walk from the boardwalk and close to plenty of shops. Thanks again guys, we won't forget it!!</review>

<time>1427656205545</time><username>Demetra George< /username><user_id>105111377866776879659</user_id>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>
<Review>We have stayed here twice now and there is one main point the negative reviewers keep forgetting to mention: **affordable** views.  That, and kind/competent staff, is what brought us back to the Casablanca.

The Casablanca has the absolute best location and views on the beach.  If you don't believe me, ask them to take a look at room 15A, which is where we spent the better part of last week (3/23/15-3/26/15).  From our room, we could see everything from Lighthouse Field State Beach, to the Municipal Wharf, to the Boardwalk, and all beaches, volleyball courts and palm trees in-between.  We actually went to the grocery store every day so we could have dinner in our room and watch the sunset every night because we couldn't think of anywhere in town we would have such a panoramic view.  Plus, we didn't have to take a second mortgage on our house to be able to stay here and do this.

This mansion is over 100 years old, and we personally witnessed all the upgrades the new owners are currently doing.  We originally requested the room we had last summer (#5, which is right above the beach and was absolutely fabulous), but the whole string of rooms along Beach Street, plus all the bungalows along Main Street, have been gutted and are at the end stages of a complete remodel.  Knowing we definitely wanted another view room, we were offered a few different choices, in a few different price ranges, and we were amazed at the room we received for a price that was about $30 more a night than a comparable room down the road that would've been facing the freeway.

The old saying, "You get what you pay for" doesn't apply at the Casablanca, because you get so much more.  For a very comfortable price, we had a clean room with a lovely kitchen, a fireplace nook and breathtaking views.

We will never stay anywhere else in Santa Cruz.  The Casablanca has become our home away from home.

My husband and I only have one regret about this place - we can't move in.< /Review>< response>

<rate>5</rate>< review>
This was my first time here, the entrance was a bit confusing as to where it was but the security officer helped point the direction, which was very helpful. Admission was $2.00, not bad really, they searched our bags upon entering and then stamped our hands and in we went. The place is very well kept, no junk on the walk paths to trip over or go through your shoe, they keep things picked up. There are many workers around the grounds so I imagine if you had a question they could help, we were lucky and found what we needed within the first few minutes we were there. We went and paid and were offered the option to purchase a warranty for the parts we bought, which I thought was amazing. Considering that it is a junkyard, it was a very good experience. We will return here whenever another used part is needed.<//review>

< Review>
The truth...the whole facility and yard is organized very well compared to the other dismantling companies in Fresno. It was also the cleanest, you can tell the staff runs a tight ship there. I was able to buy my engine there for less than 200 bucks which is crazy cheap instead of getting hosed somewhere else for a grand or more. The body parts there are also very cheap, so it's disturbing when I hear other customers say it's expensive there. If they went to a full service yard or a dealer they would probly have a heart attack. They also give competitive prices for junk cars too, key word in this sentence is "junk". As for the security, they are strict which is good for them. I understand it's a junk yard there are literally millions of small parts people can shove in their pockets, I didn't have a problem with it. They were very cool about it, I know it's a business, we're on private property they have every right to screen people on the way out....it's call safeguarding their business which is smart. Now I know why those idiots Pick a Part went out of business, I used to see people wall out with a lot of parts (even engines/trannys) without being paid for. The workers there didn't care. At westside auto dismantlers it's kind of cool to see a staff that takes a little pride in what they do. They do treat you fair there it's the truth, you just can't treat them like crap there because they will bounce you out I have seen it done. I recommend this place for cheap parts, my experience was good. Best auto and truck dismantling yard in Fresno/ the valley. Beautiful building and office too, would of never thought it was a wrecking yard from the outside compared to alot of the other dumps in Fresno. Just don't steal they will bounce you out.<//Review>

This is a very good spot to watch the sunset. I especially like early morning hikes here as well. Last time I was here I saw a pod of dolphins in the water. <gmapID>0x80deabd04f961fdf:0x8dca463a22e81674< /gmapID>< user_name>
charles chiles<//user_name>
<user_id>115802051008320845898<//user_id>< Resp>
None< /Resp>
< text>
Luscomb's Point is a nice place to watch a beautiful San Diego sunset. It is accessible via Sunset Cliffs Drive-south-from the I-8 Freeway west and also by taking the bridge (south) across the flood control channel ( You follow Sunset Cliffs Drive southward, straight through Ocean Beach and Luscomb's Point is a very large dirt lot, bordered on the east side of Sunset Cliffs Drive by the upscale Pt. Loma and beachfront homes.
The only parking is curbside and on a nice day it's often difficult to find a parking space without a short walk.
Luscomb's Point is well known as one of Sunset Cliffs premier righthand surf points; the bottom consists of flat rocky reef.
On a very good day, when the winter swells are out of the west or northwest and about 4' to 8,' this area produces some very nice righthanders : It's at it's very best between 6' to 8' with an occasional 10' beauty.
It's usually best when it's glassy or slightly windblown however, it can also get quite crowded; when it's at it's hot, it should be surfed by only very experienced surfers.
The crowd can also get quite aggressive but, surfing etiquette prevails.
It's best surfed at a medium to low tide, with the very low tides producing some extremely steep drops, walls and an occasional tube. The medium tides producing some long walls and nice off the lip rides ; if you can make it around an occasional inside wall, the ride is quite long.
It's also a good place for photographers, because the break is closer to the rocky shoreline.
When paddling out, it's fairly easy unless you get directly in front of the rocky wall when the sets are big and the tide is a little higher however, there are several good entry and exit spots.
It's also a shortboarder's wave. If you have a longboard, try North Garbage and other slower areas.
The best months are usually December through mid February. In the summer it's usually flat in this area.</text>
